      DO DFDELETE("cad",">");
      DO DFCOPY'F ("bdd","cad");

		tx_mp3m_dai :  tx_mp3m_dai = td_mp3m_dai3 / (td_p4m_dai3 - td_mp3m_dai3) ,
		tx_mp3m_dsa :  tx_mp3m_dsa = td_mp3m_dsa3 / (td_p4m_dsa3 - td_mp3m_dsa3) ,
		tx_mp3m_dse :  tx_mp3m_dse = td_mp3m_dse3 / (td_p4m_dse3 - td_mp3m_dse3) ,
		tx_mp3m_nrj :  tx_mp3m_nrj = td_mp3m_nrj3 / (td_p4m_nrj3 - td_mp3m_nrj3) ,

	// TVA et marges par opération
		td_mp3m_dai7_ch : td_mp3m_dai7_ch = ct_mp3m_dai7_ch * td_p4m_dai7_ch ,
		td_mp3m_dai9_ch : td_mp3m_dai9_ch = ct_mp3m_dai9_ch * td_p4m_dai9_ch ,
		td_mp3m_dse7_ch : td_mp3m_dse7_ch = ct_mp3m_dse7_ch * td_p4m_dse7_ch ,
		td_mp3m_dse9_ch : td_mp3m_dse9_ch = ct_mp3m_dse9_ch * td_p4m_dse9_ch ,
		td_mp3m_nrj7_ch : td_mp3m_nrj7_ch = ct_mp3m_nrj7_ch * td_p4m_nrj7_ch ,
		td_mp3m_nrj9_ch : td_mp3m_nrj9_ch = ct_mp3m_nrj9_ch * td_p4m_nrj9_ch ,
		td_mp2_dai7_ch  : td_mp2_dai7_ch  = ct_mp2_dai7_ch  * td_p2_dai7_ch  ,
		td_mp2_dai9_ch  : td_mp2_dai9_ch  = ct_mp2_dai9_ch  * td_p2_dai9_ch  ,
		td_mp2_dse7_ch  : td_mp2_dse7_ch  = ct_mp2_dse7_ch  * td_p2_dse7_ch  ,
		td_mp2_dse9_ch  : td_mp2_dse9_ch  = ct_mp2_dse9_ch  * td_p2_dse9_ch  ,
		td_mp2_nrj7_ch  : td_mp2_nrj7_ch  = ct_mp2_nrj7_ch  * td_p2_nrj7_ch  ,
		td_mp2_nrj9_ch  : td_mp2_nrj9_ch  = ct_mp2_nrj9_ch  * td_p2_nrj9_ch  ,
		td_mp51_dai7_ch : td_mp51_dai7_ch = ct_mp51_dai7_ch * td_p51_dai7_ch ,
		td_mp51_dai9_ch : td_mp51_dai9_ch = ct_mp51_dai9_ch * td_p51_dai9_ch ,
		td_mp6_dai7_ch : td_mp6_dai7_ch = ct_mp6_dai7_ch * td_p4m_dai7_ch ,
		td_mp6_dai9_ch : td_mp6_dai9_ch = ct_mp6_dai9_ch * td_p4m_dai9_ch ,
		td_mp6_dse7_ch : td_mp6_dse7_ch = ct_mp6_dse7_ch * td_p4m_dse7_ch ,
		td_mp6_dse9_ch : td_mp6_dse9_ch = ct_mp6_dse9_ch * td_p4m_dse9_ch ,
		td_mp6_nrj7_ch : td_mp6_nrj7_ch = ct_mp6_nrj7_ch * td_p4m_nrj7_ch ,
		td_mp6_nrj9_ch : td_mp6_nrj9_ch = ct_mp6_nrj9_ch * td_p4m_nrj9_ch ,
		
		td_vp4m_dai3    : td_vp4m_dai3    = ct_vp4m_dai3 * td_p4m_dai3,
		td_vp4m_dai7_ch : td_vp4m_dai7_ch = ct_vp4m_dai7_ch * td_p4m_dai7_ch,
		td_vp4m_dse3    : td_vp4m_dse3    = ct_vp4m_dse3 * td_p4m_dse3,
		td_vp4m_dse7_ch : td_vp4m_dse7_ch = ct_vp4m_dse7_ch * td_p4m_dse7_ch,
		td_vp4m_dsa3    : td_vp4m_dsa3    = ct_vp4m_dsa3 * td_p4m_dsa3,
		td_vp4m_dsa7_ch : td_vp4m_dsa7_ch = ct_vp4m_dsa7_ch * td_p4m_dsa7_ch,
		td_vp4m_dsn3    : td_vp4m_dsn3    = ct_vp4m_dsn3 * td_p4m_dsn3,
		td_vp4m_dsn7_ch : td_vp4m_dsn7_ch = ct_vp4m_dsn7_ch * td_p4m_dsn7_ch,
		td_vp4m_nrj3    : td_vp4m_nrj3    = ct_vp4m_nrj3 * td_p4m_nrj3,
		td_vp4m_nrj7_ch : td_vp4m_nrj7_ch = ct_vp4m_nrj7_ch * td_p4m_nrj7_ch,
		td_vp2_dai3 	 : td_vp2_dai3     = ct_vp2_dai3 * td_p2_dai3,
		td_vp2_dai7_ch  : td_vp2_dai7_ch  = ct_vp2_dai7_ch * td_p2_dai7_ch,
		td_vp2_dse3 	 : td_vp2_dse3     = ct_vp2_dse3 * td_p2_dse3,
		td_vp2_dse7_ch  : td_vp2_dse7_ch  = ct_vp2_dse7_ch * td_p2_dse7_ch,
		td_vp2_dsa3 	 : td_vp2_dsa3     = ct_vp2_dsa3 * td_p2_dsa3,
		td_vp2_dsa7_ch  : td_vp2_dsa7_ch  = ct_vp2_dsa7_ch * td_p2_dsa7_ch,
		td_vp2_dsn3 	 : td_vp2_dsn3     = ct_vp2_dsn3 * td_p2_dsn3,
		td_vp2_dsn7_ch  : td_vp2_dsn7_ch  = ct_vp2_dsn7_ch * td_p2_dsn7_ch,
		td_vp2_nrj3 	 : td_vp2_nrj3     = ct_vp2_nrj3 * td_p2_nrj3,
		td_vp2_nrj7_ch  : td_vp2_nrj7_ch  = ct_vp2_nrj7_ch * td_p2_nrj7_ch,
		td_vp51_dai3 	 : td_vp51_dai3    = ct_vp51_dai3 * td_p51_dai3,
		td_vp51_dai7_ch : td_vp51_dai7_ch = ct_vp51_dai7_ch * td_p51_dai7_ch,
		td_vp51_dse3 	 : td_vp51_dse3    = ct_vp51_dse3 * td_p51_dse3,
		td_vp51_dse7_ch : td_vp51_dse7_ch = ct_vp51_dse7_ch * td_p51_dse7_ch,
		td_vp51_dsa3 	 : td_vp51_dsa3    = ct_vp51_dsa3 * td_p51_dsa3,
		td_vp51_dsa7_ch : td_vp51_dsa7_ch = ct_vp51_dsa7_ch * td_p51_dsa7_ch,
		
		//transferts de passage branche-produit pour la production
		td_p1e_dai3 : td_p1e_dai3 = td_p1_dai3 - td_tr_dai3 , 
		td_p1e_dai7 : td_p1e_dai7 = td_p1_dai7 - td_tr_dai7 , 
		td_p1e_dsa3 : td_p1e_dsa3 = td_p1_dsa3 - td_tr_dsa3 , 
		td_p1e_dsa7 : td_p1e_dsa7 = td_p1_dsa7 - td_tr_dsa7 , 
		td_p1e_dse3 : td_p1e_dse3 = td_p1_dse3 - td_tr_dse3 , 
		td_p1e_dse7 : td_p1e_dse7 = td_p1_dse7 - td_tr_dse7 , 
		td_p1e_nrj3 : td_p1e_nrj3 = td_p1_nrj3 - td_tr_nrj3 , 
		td_p1e_nrj7 : td_p1e_nrj7 = td_p1_nrj7 - td_tr_nrj7 , 
		td_p1e_dsn3 : td_p1e_dsn3 = td_p1_dsn3 - td_tr_dsn3 , 
		td_p1e_dsn7 : td_p1e_dsn7 = td_p1_dsn7 - td_tr_dsn7 ,
		td_p1e_dhnrj3 :  td_p1e_dhnrj3 = td_p1e_d3 - td_p1e_nrj3 , 
		td_p1e_dhnrj7 : td_p1e_dhnrj7 = td_p1e_d7 - td_p1e_nrj7 , 
		//solde sur dsn
		td_tr_dsn3 : td_tr_nrj3 + td_tr_dai3 + td_tr_dsa3 + td_tr_dse3 + td_tr_dsn3 = 0 ,
		td_tr_dsn7 : td_tr_nrj7 + td_tr_dai7 + td_tr_dsa7 + td_tr_dse7 + td_tr_dsn7 = 0 ,
		
		td_p1e_d7 : td_p1e_d7 = td_p1e_dai7 + td_p1e_dse7 + td_p1e_dsa7 + td_p1e_dsn7 + td_p1e_nrj7,
		td_p1e_d3 : td_p1e_d3 = td_p1e_dai3 + td_p1e_dse3 + td_p1e_dsa3 + td_p1e_dsn3 + td_p1e_nrj3,

     // 2b - équations comptables du tee
         // par branche 
	      tc_d29_d3 : tc_d29_d3 = tc_d29_dai3 + tc_d29_dse3 + tc_d29_dsa3 + tc_d29_dsn3 + tc_d29_nrj3 , 
          tc_d39_d3 : tc_d39_d3 = tc_d39_dai3 + tc_d39_dse3 + tc_d39_dsa3 + tc_d39_dsn3 + tc_d39_nrj3 ,
          
          			
     // 2c - lien entre tes et tee
	   // pib, pibhs, b1
		  td_pib3        : td_pib3   = td_p3_d3+td_p51_d3+td_p54_d3+td_p6_d3-td_p7_d3 ,
		  td_pib7        : td_pib7   = td_p3_d7+td_p51_d7+td_p54_d7+td_p6_d7-td_p7_d7  ,
		  
		  td_pibhs3      : td_pibhs3 = td_pib3 - td_p54_d3 ,
		  td_pibhs7      : td_pibhs7 = td_pib7 - td_p54_d7 ,		  
		  
		  td_b1_d3       : td_b1_d3    = td_p1e_d3   - td_p2e_d3   ,
		  td_b1_d7       : td_b1_d7    = td_p1e_d7   - td_p2e_d7   ,
		  td_b1_dai3     : td_b1_dai3  = td_p1e_dai3 - td_p2e_dai3 ,
		  td_b1_dai7     : td_b1_dai7  = td_p1e_dai7 - td_p2e_dai7 ,
		  td_b1_nrj3     : td_b1_nrj3  = td_p1e_nrj3 - td_p2e_nrj3 ,
		  td_b1_nrj7     : td_b1_nrj7  = td_p1e_nrj7 - td_p2e_nrj7 ,
		  td_b1_dse3     : td_b1_dse3  = td_p1e_dse3 - td_p2e_dse3 ,
		  td_b1_dse7     : td_b1_dse7  = td_p1e_dse7 - td_p2e_dse7 ,
		  td_b1_dsa3     : td_b1_dsa3  = td_p1e_dsa3 - td_p2e_dsa3 ,
		  td_b1_dsa7     : td_b1_dsa7  = td_p1e_dsa7 - td_p2e_dsa7 ,
		  td_b1_dsn3     : td_b1_dsn3  = td_p1e_dsn3 - td_p2e_dsn3 ,
		  td_b1_dsn7     : td_b1_dsn7  = td_p1e_dsn7 - td_p2e_dsn7 ,

		  td_b1_sm3      : td_b1_sm3   = td_b1_dai3 + td_b1_nrj3 + td_b1_dse3 + td_b1_dsa3 ,
		  td_b1_sm7      : td_b1_sm7   = td_b1_dai7 + td_b1_nrj7 + td_b1_dse7 + td_b1_dsa7 ,
		  
		  td_b1_dhnrj3 :  td_b1_dhnrj3 = td_b1_d3 - td_b1_nrj3 ,
		  td_b1_dhnrj7 : td_b1_dhnrj7 = td_b1_d7 - td_b1_nrj7 ,
		  
     // 2d - marché du travail, du capital (marché du travail dans le fichier mes3b)
		  tc_d12_d3 	 : tc_d12_d3    = tc_d1_d3-tc_d11_d3 ,
          
          tcs : tcs = tcs_nq*tc_d11_nq3/tc_d11_s14r3 + tcs_q*tc_d11_q3/tc_d11_s14r3 + tcsdsn*tc_d11_dsn3/tc_d11_s14r3 + tcsrdm*(tc_d11_s2e3-tc_d11_s2r3)/tc_d11_s14r3 + tcs_cale, 
		  csgcrds : csgcrds = tcsg_trav + tcrds_trav + csgcrds_cale,
          
          ck          : ck   = td_p51s_d9_ch  *(oat10a+tdec  +prime+fisc-(td_p51s_d9_ch  /td_p51s_d9_ch(-4)  -1)*100)/100,
          ck1 		  : ck1  = td_p51s_d9_ch*(oat10a+tdec  +prime+fisc1-(td_p51s_d9_ch  /td_p51s_d9_ch(-4)  -1)*100)/100 ,
          
          
          ck_dai      : ck_dai=td_p51s_dai9_ch*(oat10a+tdec_dai+prime+fisc-(td_p51s_dai9_ch/td_p51s_dai9_ch(-4)-1)*100)/100,
          ck_dse      : ck_dse=td_p51s_dse9_ch*(oat10a+tdec_dse+prime+fisc-(td_p51s_dse9_ch/td_p51s_dse9_ch(-4)-1)*100)/100,
          ck_dsa      : ck_dsa=td_p51s_dsa9_ch*(oat10a+tdec_dsa+prime+fisc-(td_p51s_dsa9_ch/td_p51s_dsa9_ch(-4)-1)*100)/100,

          ckr_sm      : ckr_sm   =ck/td_b1_sm9_ch ,
          ckr_d       : ckr_d   =ck/td_b1_d9_ch ,
        

          knet        : knet  =(1-tdec3/4)*knet(-1)+td_p51s_d3/1000,
       	  knetvol     : knetvol  =(1-tdec3/4)*knetvol(-1)+td_p51s_d7_ch/1000,
       	  
     // 2e - autres équations comptables 
		  	// variables pour com ext		  
		  compet_prix_dai : compet_prix_dai = petx/td_p6_dai9_ch/100,
		  compet_prix_dse : compet_prix_dse = petx/td_p6_dse9_ch/100,
		  csu_d 		 : csu_d = tc_d1_d3 / td_pib7_ch * 100 , 
		  compet_cout : compet_cout = num_comp_cout / csu_d / 100 ,


	      tuc     : LOG(tuc)   = LOG(prodk) + (1/0.38) * LOG(td_b1_sm7_ch) - (0.62/0.38) * (LOG(tc_emps_sm7)+Eff2) - LOG(knetvol(-1)),

		  
		  eur3m  	: eur3m = eur3mr + inflation ,
          oat10a		: oat10a = oat10ar + (td_p51s_d9_ch/td_p51s_d9_ch(-4)-1)*100 ,
          compit_dse : compit_dse = td_p7_dse9_ch/td_p1_dse9_ch ,
          

          baril		: baril = baril_us*usa_tc ,
          
          
     // 3a - coefficients techniques du tes
			// les marges de transport indexées sur P1 + P7 ; DSE en solde
		  td_temp_dai3	 : td_temp_dai3    = ct_temp_dai3 * td_rntpp_dai3 ,  
		  td_temp_dai7	 : td_temp_dai7_ch = ct_temp_dai7 * td_rntpp_dai7_ch ,
		  td_temp_nrj3	 : td_temp_nrj3    = ct_temp_nrj3 * td_rntpp_nrj3 ,
		  td_temp_nrj7	 : td_temp_nrj7_ch = ct_temp_nrj7 * td_rntpp_nrj7_ch ,
		  td_temp_dse3   : 0 = td_temp_dai3+td_temp_dse3+td_temp_nrj3,
		  td_temp_dse7   : 0 = td_temp_dai7+td_temp_dse7+td_temp_nrj7,
     
    	  tx_temp_dai : tx_temp_dai = td_temp_dai3 / td_rntpp_dai3,
		  tx_temp_nrj : tx_temp_nrj = td_temp_nrj3 / td_rntpp_nrj3,
		  tx_temp_dse : tx_temp_dse = td_temp_dse3 / td_rntpp_dse3, 

           // impôts sur les importations 
          td_d212_dai3	 : td_d212_dai3 	= ct_d212_dai3 * td_p7_dai3 ,    
		  td_d212_dai7	 : td_d212_dai7_ch  = ct_d212_dai7 * td_p7_dai7_ch ,
	      td_d212_nrj3	 : td_d212_nrj3 	= ct_d212_nrj3 * td_p7_nrj3 ,
		  td_d212_nrj7	 : td_d212_nrj7_ch  = ct_d212_nrj7 * td_p7_nrj7_ch ,
		  td_d212_dse3	 : td_d212_dse3 	= ct_d212_dse3 * td_p7_dse3 ,
		  td_d212_dse7	 : td_d212_dse7_ch  = ct_d212_dse7 * td_p7_dse7_ch ,
          
          tx_d212_dai : tx_d212_dai = td_d212_dai3 / td_p7_dai3 ,
		  tx_d212_dse : tx_d212_dse = td_d212_dse3 / td_p7_dse3 ,
		  tx_d212_nrj : tx_d212_nrj = td_d212_nrj3 / td_p7_nrj3 ,
	
          // autres impôts sur les produits
		  td_d214_dai3 : td_d214_dai3 = ct_d214_dai3 * (td_p3m_dai3/(1+tx_vp4m_dai)), 
		  td_d214_dse3 : td_d214_dse3 = ct_d214_dse3 * (td_p3m_dse3/(1+tx_vp4m_dse)),
		  td_d214_dsa3 : td_d214_dsa3 = ct_d214_dsa3 * (td_p3m_dsa3/(1+tx_vp4m_dsa)),
		  
		  td_d214_dai7 : td_d214_dai7_ch = ct_d214_dai7 * (td_p3m_dai7_ch /(1+td_vp4m_dai7_ch / (td_p4m_dai7_ch-td_vp4m_dai7_ch)))    , 
		  td_d214_dse7 : td_d214_dse7_ch = ct_d214_dse7 * (td_p3m_dse7_ch/(1+td_vp4m_dse7_ch / (td_p4m_dse7_ch-td_vp4m_dse7_ch)))     ,
		  td_d214_dsa7 : td_d214_dsa7_ch = ct_d214_dsa7 * (td_p3m_dsa7_ch/(1+td_vp4m_dsa7_ch / (td_p4m_dsa7_ch-td_vp4m_dsa7_ch)))     ,
		  td_d214_nrj7 : td_d214_nrj7_ch = ct_d214_nrj7 * ((td_p2dhnrj_nrj7_ch + td_p3m_nrj7_ch)/(1+td_vp4m_nrj7_ch / (td_p4m_nrj7_ch-td_vp4m_nrj7_ch)))  , 
			

		  tx_d214_dai : tx_d214_dai = td_d214_dai3 / (td_p3m_dai3/(1+tx_vp4m_dai)), 
		  tx_d214_dse : tx_d214_dse = td_d214_dse3 / (td_p3m_dse3/(1+tx_vp4m_dse)),
		  tx_d214_dsa : tx_d214_dsa = td_d214_dsa3 / (td_p3m_dsa3/(1+tx_vp4m_dsa)),
		  tx_d214_nrj : tx_d214_nrj = td_d214_nrj3 /((td_p2dhnrj_nrj7_ch + td_p3m_nrj7_ch)/(1+tx_vp4m_nrj)),
	
		  // subventions sur les produits
		  td_d319_dai3 : td_d319_dai3 = ct_d319_dai3 * td_p1_dai3,     
		  td_d319_dse3 : td_d319_dse3 = ct_d319_dse3 * td_p1_dse3,
		  td_d319_dsa3 : td_d319_dsa3 = ct_d319_dsa3 * td_p1_dsa3,
		  td_d319_nrj3 : td_d319_nrj3 = ct_d319_nrj3 * td_p1_nrj3,
	
		  td_d319_dai7 : td_d319_dai7_ch = ct_d319_dai7 * td_p1_dai7_ch,   
		  td_d319_dse7 : td_d319_dse7_ch = ct_d319_dse7 * td_p1_dse7_ch,
		  td_d319_dsa7 : td_d319_dsa7_ch = ct_d319_dsa7 * td_p1_dsa7_ch,
		  td_d319_nrj7 : td_d319_nrj7_ch = ct_d319_nrj7 * td_p1_nrj7_ch,
	
		  tx_d319_dai : tx_d319_dai = td_d319_dai3 / td_p1_dai3 ,
		  tx_d319_dse : tx_d319_dse = td_d319_dse3 / td_p1_dse3 ,
		  tx_d319_dsa : tx_d319_dsa = td_d319_dsa3 / td_p1_dsa3 ,
		  tx_d319_nrj : tx_d319_nrj = td_d319_nrj3 / td_p1_nrj3 ,
		  tx_d319_dsn : tx_d319_dsn = td_d319_dsn3 / td_p1_dsn3 , 
	

td_p2dai_dai3 : td_p2dai_dai3 = td_p2dai_dai7_ch * td_p2_dai9_ch/100 * ct_p2dai_dai3 ,
td_p2dai_nrj3 : td_p2dai_nrj3 = td_p2dai_nrj7_ch * td_p2_nrj9_ch/100 * ct_p2dai_nrj3 ,
td_p2dai_dse3 : td_p2dai_dse3 = td_p2dai_dse7_ch * td_p2_dse9_ch/100 * ct_p2dai_dse3 ,
td_p2dai_dsa3 : td_p2dai_dsa3 = td_p2dai_dsa7_ch * td_p2_dsa9_ch/100 * ct_p2dai_dsa3 ,
td_p2dai_dsn3 : td_p2dai_dsn3 = td_p2dai_dsn7_ch * td_p2_dsn9_ch/100 * ct_p2dai_dsn3 ,
td_p2nrj_dai3 : td_p2nrj_dai3 = td_p2nrj_dai7_ch * td_p2_dai9_ch/100 * ct_p2nrj_dai3 ,
td_p2nrj_nrj3 : td_p2nrj_nrj3 = td_p2nrj_nrj7_ch * td_p2_nrj9_ch/100 * ct_p2nrj_nrj3 ,
td_p2nrj_dse3 : td_p2nrj_dse3 = td_p2nrj_dse7_ch * td_p2_dse9_ch/100 * ct_p2nrj_dse3 ,
td_p2nrj_dsa3 : td_p2nrj_dsa3 = td_p2nrj_dsa7_ch * td_p2_dsa9_ch/100 * ct_p2nrj_dsa3 ,
td_p2nrj_dsn3 : td_p2nrj_dsn3 = td_p2nrj_dsn7_ch * td_p2_dsn9_ch/100 * ct_p2nrj_dsn3 ,
td_p2dse_dai3 : td_p2dse_dai3 = td_p2dse_dai7_ch * td_p2_dai9_ch/100 * ct_p2dse_dai3 ,
td_p2dse_nrj3 : td_p2dse_nrj3 = td_p2dse_nrj7_ch * td_p2_nrj9_ch/100 * ct_p2dse_nrj3 ,
td_p2dse_dse3 : td_p2dse_dse3 = td_p2dse_dse7_ch * td_p2_dse9_ch/100 * ct_p2dse_dse3 ,
td_p2dse_dsa3 : td_p2dse_dsa3 = td_p2dse_dsa7_ch * td_p2_dsa9_ch/100 * ct_p2dse_dsa3 ,
td_p2dse_dsn3 : td_p2dse_dsn3 = td_p2dse_dsn7_ch * td_p2_dsn9_ch/100 * ct_p2dse_dsn3 ,
td_p2dsa_dai3 : td_p2dsa_dai3 = td_p2dsa_dai7_ch * td_p2_dai9_ch/100 * ct_p2dsa_dai3 ,
td_p2dsa_nrj3 : td_p2dsa_nrj3 = td_p2dsa_nrj7_ch * td_p2_nrj9_ch/100 * ct_p2dsa_nrj3 ,
td_p2dsa_dse3 : td_p2dsa_dse3 = td_p2dsa_dse7_ch * td_p2_dse9_ch/100 * ct_p2dsa_dse3 ,
td_p2dsa_dsa3 : td_p2dsa_dsa3 = td_p2dsa_dsa7_ch * td_p2_dsa9_ch/100 * ct_p2dsa_dsa3 ,
td_p2dsa_dsn3 : td_p2dsa_dsn3 = td_p2dsa_dsn7_ch * td_p2_dsn9_ch/100 * ct_p2dsa_dsn3 ,

td_p2dai_dsn7_ch : td_p2dai_dsn7_ch = ct_p2dai_dsn7_ch * td_p1e_dai7_ch ,
td_p2dse_dai7_ch : td_p2dse_dai7_ch = ct_p2dse_dai7_ch * td_p1e_dse7_ch ,

td_p2dse_dsa7_ch : td_p2dse_dsa7_ch = ct_p2dse_dsa7_ch * td_p1e_dse7_ch ,
td_p2dse_dsn7_ch : td_p2dse_dsn7_ch = ct_p2dse_dsn7_ch * td_p1e_dse7_ch ,
td_p2dsa_dai7_ch : td_p2dsa_dai7_ch = ct_p2dsa_dai7_ch * td_p1e_dsa7_ch ,
td_p2dsa_dse7_ch : td_p2dsa_dse7_ch = ct_p2dsa_dse7_ch * td_p1e_dsa7_ch ,

// cas spécifique des volumes de CI en NRJ :
td_p2dai_nrj7     : td_p2dai_nrj7    = td_p2dhnrj_nrj7  - td_p2dse_nrj7 -td_p2dsa_nrj7 - td_p2dsn_nrj7  ,
td_p2dse_nrj7_ch : td_p2dse_nrj7_ch = ct_p2dse_nrj7_ch * td_p2dhnrj_nrj7_ch ,

          // prix CI
          

 td_p2_dai9_ch : td_p2_dai9_ch = ct_p2_dai9_ch
						*(1+tx_vp2_dai)*(1+tx_d214_dai)*(1+tx_temp_dai)
						*td_rntpp_dai9_ch ,


 td_p2_dse9_ch : td_p2_dse9_ch = ct_p2_dse9_ch
						*(1+tx_vp2_dse)*(1+tx_d214_dse)*(1+tx_temp_dse)
						*td_rntpp_dse9_ch ,


 td_p2_dsa9_ch : td_p2_dsa9_ch = ct_p2_dsa9_ch
						*(1+tx_vp2_dsa)*(1+tx_d214_dsa) 
						*td_rntpp_dsa9_ch,

   
	// prix CI NRJ : champ "toute économie hors branche énergie" 
 td_p2dhnrj_nrj9_ch : td_p2dhnrj_nrj9_ch/(1+tx_vp2_nrj)-(td_d214_nrj7_ch/(td_p2_nrj7_ch+td_p3m_nrj7_ch))*td_d214_nrj9_ch = ct_p2dhnrj_nrj9_ch 
					*(1+tx_temp_nrj)
						*td_rntpp_nrj9_ch,



	
	// prix de consommation des ménages
	
	
 td_p3m_dai9_ch : td_p3m_dai9_ch = c_p3m_dai9_ch
						*(1+tx_vp4m_dai)*(1+tx_d214_dai)*(1+tx_temp_dai)
						*td_rntpp_dai9_ch,


 td_p3m_dse9_ch : td_p3m_dse9_ch = c_p3m_dse9_ch
						*(1+tx_vp4m_dse)*(1+tx_d214_dse)*(1+tx_temp_dse)
						*td_rntpp_dse9_ch,

 
 td_p3m_nrj9_ch  : td_p3m_nrj9_ch/(1+tx_vp4m_nrj)-(td_d214_nrj7_ch/(td_p2_nrj7_ch+td_p3m_nrj7_ch))*td_d214_nrj9_ch =ct_p3m_nrj9_ch
						*td_rntpp_nrj9_ch,


 td_p3m_dsa9_ch : td_p3m_dsa9_ch = c_p3m_dsa9_ch
						*(1+tx_vp4m_dsa)*(1+tx_d214_dsa) 
						*td_rntpp_dsa9_ch,


						//Prix d'investissement
 td_p51s_dai9_ch : td_p51s_dai9_ch = ct_p51s_dai9_ch

						*(1+tx_d319_dai)*td_p1_ycmg_dai9_ch,


 td_p51s_dse9_ch : td_p51s_dse9_ch = ct_p51s_dse9_ch
						*(1+tx_vp51_dse)*(1+tx_d214_dse)*(1+tx_temp_dse)
						*(1+tx_d319_dse) *td_p1_ycmg_dse9_ch,


 td_p51s_dsa9_ch : td_p51s_dsa9_ch = ct_p51s_dsa9_ch
						*(1+tx_vp51_dsa)*(1+tx_d214_dsa)
						*(1+tx_d319_dsa) *td_p1_ycmg_dsa9_ch,

 
 td_p51m_dse9_ch : td_p51m_dse9_ch = ct_p51m_dse9_ch
	   						*(1+tx_vp51_dse)*(1+tx_d214_dse)*(1+tx_temp_dse)
	   						*td_rntpp_dse9_ch,

	   						*(1+tx_vp51_dsa)*(1+tx_d214_dsa)
	   						*td_rntpp_dsa9_ch,


	
c_p3m_dai9_ch : LOG(c_p3m_dai9_ch)-c_p3m_dai9_cale=cp3mdai9const'c,

c_p3m_dse9_ch : LOG(c_p3m_dse9_ch)-c_p3m_dse9_cale=cp3mdse9const'c,								

c_p3m_dsa9_ch : LOG(c_p3m_dsa9_ch)-c_p3m_dsa9_cale=cp3mdsa9const'c,


       

  	  tei_pconso_pva : tei_pconso_pva = td_p3m_d9_ch / td_b1_sm9_ch , 
      tei_pinv_pva 	 : tei_pinv_pva   = td_p51s_d9_ch / td_b1_sm9_ch ,

 	 // prix dsn :
		td_p3m_dsn9_ch : td_p3m_dsn9_ch = ct_p3m_dsn9_ch * td_p1_dsn9_ch    , 
		td_p2_dsn9_ch  : td_p2_dsn9_ch  = ct_p2_dsn9_ch  *  td_p1_dsn9_ch	 ,   	   
	
	    td_b1_dsn9_ch : td_b1_dsn9_ch = ct_b1_dsn9_ch *  smpt_dsn/(EXP(eff_dsn))  , 
	    eff_dsn : DEL(eff_dsn) - DEL(ct_eff_dsn) = -0.1*(eff_dsn - ct_eff_dsn -  eff2)(-1)  ,
	    td_b1_dsn7_ch : td_b1_dsn7_ch = ct_b1_dsn7_ch* tc_emps_dsn1*(EXP(eff_dsn)),

    ecm_d62hcho_s13e3: DEL(LOG(tc_d62hcho_s13e3)-d62hcho_cale) = 
						d62hcho_s13e3c'c
						+ d62hcho_s13e3pi'c  * 1/4 * DEL(4:LOG(ipc))(-4)
						+d62hcho_s13e3mu'c*(LOG(tc_d62hcho_s13e3/td_p3m_d9_ch)-d62hcho_cale)(-1)
						+d62hcho_s13e3mutr'c*temps80(-1) ,
    
   
   ;
	 FILEMOD mesangehorsML ;
	 ACCESS cad     type formdata id .\bdd\don3a.frm         mode w; SEARCH cad;
     ACCESS coefmod type formdata id .\bdd\mesangecoefhorsML.frm mode w; SEARCH coefmod;
	 
    // ***********************************************************************************************************************
    // ***** mise à 0 des cales et des coefficients techniques                                                           *****
    // ***********************************************************************************************************************
     DO liste_pol = MODSYM("'pol"); DO PRT.(liste_pol);
     &execmd " do cad_@(liste_pol)     = 0 * cad_td_pib3" ";" ;

    // ***********************************************************************************************************************
    // *****test modèle : lkord et &lklimit                                                                              *****
    // ***********************************************************************************************************************
     LKORD ;
     USEMOD mesangehorsML;
     &lklimit; 
    
    // ***********************************************************************************************************************
    // ***** estimation des équations                                                                                    *****
    // ***********************************************************************************************************************
    DELACCESS all; DELSAVE ; DRANGE;
    ACCESS cad     type formdata id .\bdd\don3a.frm mode r ;         SEARCH cad ;
    ACCESS coefmod type formdata id .\bdd\mesangecoefhorsML.frm mode w ; SEARCH coefmod ;

    USEMOD mesangehorsML;

	       
	// inflation - déflateur de la consommation des ménages
       BOUNDS 1984q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ipc;        FILECOEF coefmod;
    
    // ecm de prix : prix de production
       BOUNDS 1985q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p1_dai9_ch; FILECOEF coefmod; 
	   BOUNDS 1985q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p1_dse9_ch; FILECOEF coefmod;
	   BOUNDS 1985q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p1_dsa9_ch; FILECOEF coefmod;
 	   BOUNDS 1985q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p1_nrj9_ch; FILECOEF coefmod;
	
// coefficient technique P3M hors NRJ,P3G et p51 endogènes 
	   BOUNDS 1992q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD c_p3m_dai9_ch; FILECOEF coefmod; 
	   BOUNDS 1992q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD c_p3m_dse9_ch; FILECOEF coefmod; 
	   BOUNDS 1992q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD c_p3m_dsa9_ch; FILECOEF coefmod; 	   
	
	   
	 // ecm de prix : prix de commerce extérieur
	   BOUNDS 1998q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p6_dai9_ch; FILECOEF coefmod ; 
	   BOUNDS 1995q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p6_dse9_ch; FILECOEF coefmod ;
	   BOUNDS 1985q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p6_nrj9_ch; FILECOEF coefmod ;
		  
	   BOUNDS 1990q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p7_dai9_ch; FILECOEF coefmod ; 
	   BOUNDS 2003q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p7_dse9_ch; FILECOEF coefmod ;
	   BOUNDS 1985q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p7_nrj9_ch; FILECOEF coefmod ;

	// ecm de volume : demande des ménages
	   BOUNDS 1987q4 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p3m_d7_ch  ; FILECOEF coefmod;
	   BOUNDS 1985q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p3m_dai7_ch; FILECOEF coefmod;
	   BOUNDS 1986q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p3m_nrj7_ch; FILECOEF coefmod; 
	   BOUNDS 1985q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p3m_dse7_ch; FILECOEF coefmod;
	   
	
	   BOUNDS 1990q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p51m_d7_ch; FILECOEF coefmod;

	

	// ecm de volume : commerce extérieur
	   BOUNDS 1992Q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p6_dai7_ch; FILECOEF coefmod ; 
	   BOUNDS 1992Q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p6_dse7_ch; FILECOEF coefmod ;
	   BOUNDS 1985q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p6_nrj7_ch; FILECOEF coefmod ; 
	   
	   BOUNDS 1984q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p7_dai7_ch; FILECOEF coefmod ; 
	   BOUNDS 1987q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p7_dse7_ch; FILECOEF coefmod ;


	  BOUNDS 1985q1 TO 2014q2; OLSMOD ecm_p7_nrj7_ch; FILECOEF coefmod ; 

	// nrj
		BOUNDS 1990q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_p2dhnrj_nrj7_ch ; FILECOEF coefmod;
		

	   
	// autres ecm :
	   BOUNDS 1985q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_d51_s11e3; FILECOEF coefmod ; 
	   BOUNDS 1985q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_d51ir_s14e3; FILECOEF coefmod ;
	   BOUNDS  1985Q1 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ecm_d62cho_s13e3; FILECOEF coefmod ;
	   BOUNDS  1990q1 TO 2014Q4; OLSMOD ecm_d62hcho_s13e3; FILECOEF coefmod ;
	  
	  
	   BOUNDS 1983q2 TO 2014q4; OLSMOD ds_pib; FILECOEF coefmod ;

    &lklimit ;
    SIMULATE;





    // ***********************************************************************************************************************
    // ***** calcul des cales et des coefficients techniques sur le passé                                                *****
    // ***********************************************************************************************************************
    DELACCESS all; DELSAVE ; DRANGE;
    ACCESS outils id .\outils; SEARCH outils ;
    ACCESS cad     type formdata id .\bdd\don3a.frm   mode w; SEARCH cad;
    ACCESS coefmod type formdata id .\bdd\mesangecoefhorsML.frm mode r ; SEARCH coefmod ;        
      
	// création du modèle inverse
       USEMOD mesangehorsML ;
       DO PRT.(endo_ct_ecm) ; 
       &execmd "changesym exogenous @(endo_ct_ecm) ;";
       CHANGESYM endogenous >_cale ct_> tcsg_trav tcrds_trav tcsg_cap tcrds_cap ; 
	   FILEMOD invmesange ;
	   LKORD ;     

    // calage
	   USEMOD invmesange;
	   &lklimit;
	   SIMULATE;
	   CONOPT concr 0.00000000001 stop 15000;  
	   SIMSTART 1992q1 from 1980q1; DOTIL 2014q4; 
	   SAVESIM out ;
	   &execmd " do cad_@(liste_pol) = out_@(liste_pol)" ";" ; 
       DO check2'f(MODSYM("endogenous"),0.0001,"cad","out") ;  
       
	   
    // vérification du calage
       DELSAVE all ; DELACCESS all ; DRANGE ;
       ACCESS outils id .\outils; SEARCH outils ; 
       ACCESS coefmod type formdata id .\bdd\mesangecoefhorsML.frm mode r; SEARCH coefmod ;
       ACCESS cad     type formdata id .\bdd\don3a.frm mode r ;   SEARCH cad ;
       USEMOD mesangehorsML;
       &lklimit;
       SIMULATE;
       CONOPT concr 0.000000001 stop 10000;  
       SIMSTART 1992q1 from 1980q1; DOTIL 2014q4; 
       SAVESIM temp;
	   DO check2'f(MODSYM("endogenous"),0.0001,"cad","temp") ;
	   
	   DELACCESS all; DELSAVE all; DRANGE;
	  
	  /*********************************************************/
	  /******************   Fin de Mes3a        ****************/
	  /*********************************************************/
